\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ no\ 12-\/bit-\/per-\/channel\ JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ no\ JPEGs\ with\ arithmetic\ coding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ GIF\ always\ returns\ *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Basic\ usage\ (see\ HDR\ discussion\ below\ for\ HDR\ usage):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ int\ x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ unsigned\ char\ *data\ =\ stbi\_load(filename,\ \&x,\ \&y,\ \&n,\ 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ //\ ...\ process\ data\ if\ not\ NULL\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ //\ ...\ x\ =\ width,\ y\ =\ height,\ n\ =\ \#\ 8-\/bit\ components\ per\ pixel\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ //\ ...\ replace\ '0'\ with\ '1'..'4'\ to\ force\ that\ many\ components\ per\ pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ //\ ...\ but\ 'n'\ will\ always\ be\ the\ number\ that\ it\ would\ have\ been\ if\ you\ said\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Standard\ parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ int\ *x\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ outputs\ image\ width\ in\ pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ int\ *y\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ outputs\ image\ height\ in\ pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ int\ *channels\_in\_file\ \ -\/-\/\ outputs\ \#\ of\ image\ components\ in\ image\ file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ int\ desired\_channels\ \ \ -\/-\/\ if\ non-\/zero,\ \#\ of\ image\ components\ requested\ in\ result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ return\ value\ from\ an\ image\ loader\ is\ an\ 'unsigned\ char\ *'\ which\ points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ the\ pixel\ data,\ or\ NULL\ on\ an\ allocation\ failure\ or\ if\ the\ image\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00138\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ corrupt\ or\ invalid.\ The\ pixel\ data\ consists\ of\ *y\ scanlines\ of\ *x\ pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00139\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ with\ each\ pixel\ consisting\ of\ N\ interleaved\ 8-\/bit\ components;\ the\ first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ pixel\ pointed\ to\ is\ top-\/left-\/most\ in\ the\ image.\ There\ is\ no\ padding\ between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ image\ scanlines\ or\ between\ pixels,\ regardless\ of\ format.\ The\ number\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ components\ N\ is\ 'desired\_channels'\ if\ desired\_channels\ is\ non-\/zero,\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *channels\_in\_file\ otherwise.\ If\ desired\_channels\ is\ non-\/zero,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *channels\_in\_file\ has\ the\ number\ of\ components\ that\ \_would\_\ have\ been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ output\ otherwise.\ E.g.\ if\ you\ set\ desired\_channels\ to\ 4,\ you\ will\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ get\ RGBA\ output,\ but\ you\ can\ check\ *channels\_in\_file\ to\ see\ if\ it's\ trivially}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ opaque\ because\ e.g.\ there\ were\ only\ 3\ channels\ in\ the\ source\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ An\ output\ image\ with\ N\ components\ has\ the\ following\ components\ interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ this\ order\ in\ each\ pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ N=\#comp\ \ \ \ \ components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ grey,\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 3\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ red,\ green,\ blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 4\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ red,\ green,\ blue,\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ image\ loading\ fails\ for\ any\ reason,\ the\ return\ value\ will\ be\ NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ *x,\ *y,\ *channels\_in\_file\ will\ be\ unchanged.\ The\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ stbi\_failure\_reason()\ can\ be\ queried\ for\ an\ extremely\ brief,\ end-\/user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ unfriendly\ explanation\ of\ why\ the\ load\ failed.\ Define\ STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ avoid\ compiling\ these\ strings\ at\ all,\ and\ STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG\ to\ get\ slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ more\ user-\/friendly\ ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Paletted\ PNG,\ BMP,\ GIF,\ and\ PIC\ images\ are\ automatically\ depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00169\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ UNICODE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00170\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00171\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ If\ compiling\ for\ Windows\ and\ you\ wish\ to\ use\ Unicode\ filenames,\ compile}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00172\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ STBI\_WINDOWS\_UTF8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ and\ pass\ utf8-\/encoded\ filenames.\ Call\ stbi\_convert\_wchar\_to\_utf8\ to\ convert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00175\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Windows\ wchar\_t\ filenames\ to\ utf8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00176\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00177\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00178\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00179\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Philosophy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00180\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00181\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ stb\ libraries\ are\ designed\ with\ the\ following\ priorities:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00182\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00183\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ 1.\ easy\ to\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00184\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ 2.\ easy\ to\ maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00185\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ 3.\ good\ performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00186\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00187\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Sometimes\ I\ let\ "{}good\ performance"{}\ creep\ up\ in\ priority\ over\ "{}easy\ to\ maintain"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00188\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ for\ best\ performance\ I\ may\ provide\ less-\/easy-\/to-\/use\ APIs\ that\ give\ higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00189\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ performance,\ in\ addition\ to\ the\ easy-\/to-\/use\ ones.\ Nevertheless,\ it's\ important}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00190\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ keep\ in\ mind\ that\ from\ the\ standpoint\ of\ you,\ a\ client\ of\ this\ library,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00191\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ all\ you\ care\ about\ is\ \#1\ and\ \#3,\ and\ stb\ libraries\ DO\ NOT\ emphasize\ \#3\ above\ all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00192\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00193\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Some\ secondary\ priorities\ arise\ directly\ from\ the\ first\ two,\ some\ of\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00194\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ provide\ more\ explicit\ reasons\ why\ performance\ can't\ be\ emphasized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00195\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00196\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Portable\ ("{}ease\ of\ use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00197\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Small\ source\ code\ footprint\ ("{}easy\ to\ maintain"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00198\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ No\ dependencies\ ("{}ease\ of\ use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00199\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00200\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ I/O\ callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00203\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00204\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ I/O\ callbacks\ allow\ you\ to\ read\ from\ arbitrary\ sources,\ like\ packaged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00205\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ files\ or\ some\ other\ source.\ Data\ read\ from\ callbacks\ are\ processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ through\ a\ small\ internal\ buffer\ (currently\ 128\ bytes)\ to\ try\ to\ reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ three\ functions\ you\ must\ define\ are\ "{}read"{}\ (reads\ some\ bytes\ of\ data),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ "{}skip"{}\ (skips\ some\ bytes\ of\ data),\ "{}eof"{}\ (reports\ if\ the\ stream\ is\ at\ the\ end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ SIMD\ support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00215\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00216\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ JPEG\ decoder\ will\ try\ to\ automatically\ use\ SIMD\ kernels\ on\ x86\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00217\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ supported\ by\ the\ compiler.\ For\ ARM\ Neon\ support,\ you\ must\ explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00218\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ request\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00219\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00220\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (The\ old\ do-\/it-\/yourself\ SIMD\ API\ is\ no\ longer\ supported\ in\ the\ current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00221\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ code.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00222\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00223\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ On\ x86,\ SSE2\ will\ automatically\ be\ used\ when\ available\ based\ on\ a\ run-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00224\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ test;\ if\ not,\ the\ generic\ C\ versions\ are\ used\ as\ a\ fall-\/back.\ On\ ARM\ targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00225\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ typical\ path\ is\ to\ have\ separate\ builds\ for\ NEON\ and\ non-\/NEON\ devices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00226\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (at\ least\ this\ is\ true\ for\ iOS\ and\ Android).\ Therefore,\ the\ NEON\ support\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00227\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ toggled\ by\ a\ build\ flag:\ define\ STBI\_NEON\ to\ get\ NEON\ loops.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00228\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00229\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ for\ some\ reason\ you\ do\ not\ want\ to\ use\ any\ of\ SIMD\ code,\ or\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00230\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ you\ have\ issues\ compiling\ it,\ you\ can\ disable\ it\ entirely\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00231\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ defining\ STBI\_NO\_SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00232\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00233\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00234\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00235\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ HDR\ image\ support\ \ \ (disable\ by\ defining\ STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00236\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00237\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ stb\_image\ supports\ loading\ HDR\ images\ in\ general,\ and\ currently\ the\ Radiance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00238\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ .HDR\ file\ format\ specifically.\ You\ can\ still\ load\ any\ file\ through\ the\ existing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00239\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ interface;\ if\ you\ attempt\ to\ load\ an\ HDR\ file,\ it\ will\ be\ automatically\ remapped}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00240\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ LDR,\ assuming\ gamma\ 2.2\ and\ an\ arbitrary\ scale\ factor\ defaulting\ to\ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00241\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ both\ of\ these\ constants\ can\ be\ reconfigured\ through\ this\ interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00242\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00243\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00244\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00245\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00246\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (note,\ do\ not\ use\ \_inverse\_\ constants;\ stbi\_image\ will\ invert\ them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00247\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00248\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00249\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Additionally,\ there\ is\ a\ new,\ parallel\ interface\ for\ loading\ files\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00250\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (linear)\ floats\ to\ preserve\ the\ full\ dynamic\ range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00251\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00252\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ float\ *data\ =\ stbi\_loadf(filename,\ \&x,\ \&y,\ \&n,\ 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00253\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00254\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ you\ load\ LDR\ images\ through\ this\ interface,\ those\ images\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00255\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ be\ promoted\ to\ floating\ point\ values,\ run\ through\ the\ inverse\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00256\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ constants\ corresponding\ to\ the\ above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00257\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00258\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00259\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00260\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00261\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Finally,\ given\ a\ filename\ (or\ an\ open\ file\ or\ memory\ block-\/-\/see\ header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00262\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ file\ for\ details)\ containing\ image\ data,\ you\ can\ query\ for\ the\ "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00263\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ appropriate"{}\ interface\ to\ use\ (that\ is,\ whether\ the\ image\ is\ HDR\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00264\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ not),\ using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00265\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00266\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ stbi\_is\_hdr(char\ *filename);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00267\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00268\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00269\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00270\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ iPhone\ PNG\ support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00271\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00272\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ By\ default\ we\ convert\ iphone-\/formatted\ PNGs\ back\ to\ RGB,\ even\ though}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00273\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ they\ are\ internally\ encoded\ differently.\ You\ can\ disable\ this\ conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00274\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ by\ calling\ stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(0),\ in\ which\ case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00275\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ you\ will\ always\ just\ get\ the\ native\ iphone\ "{}format"{}\ through\ (which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00276\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ BGR\ stored\ in\ RGB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00277\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00278\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Call\ stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1)\ as\ well\ to\ force\ a\ divide\ per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00279\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ pixel\ to\ remove\ any\ premultiplied\ alpha\ *only*\ if\ the\ image\ file\ explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ says\ there's\ premultiplied\ data\ (currently\ only\ happens\ in\ iPhone\ images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ only\ if\ iPhone\ convert-\/to-\/rgb\ processing\ is\ on).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00282\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00283\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ===========================================================================}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00615\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET)\ \&\&\ !defined(\_\_SSE2\_\_)\ \&\&\ !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00616\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ gcc\ doesn't\ support\ sse2\ intrinsics\ unless\ you\ compile\ with\ -\/msse2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00617\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ which\ in\ turn\ means\ it\ gets\ to\ use\ SSE2\ everywhere.\ This\ is\ unfortunate,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00618\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ but\ previous\ attempts\ to\ provide\ the\ SSE2\ functions\ with\ runtime}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00619\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ detection\ caused\ numerous\ issues.\ The\ way\ architecture\ extensions\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00620\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ exposed\ in\ GCC/Clang\ is,\ sadly,\ not\ really\ suited\ for\ one-\/file\ libs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00621\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ New\ behavior:\ if\ compiled\ with\ -\/msse2,\ we\ use\ SSE2\ without\ any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00622\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ detection;\ if\ not,\ we\ don't\ use\ it\ at\ all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00623\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00624\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00625\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00626\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET)\ \&\&\ !defined(STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2)\ \&\&\ !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00627\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ \_\_MINGW32\_\_\ doesn't\ actually\ mean\ 32-\/bit,\ so\ we\ have\ to\ avoid\ STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00628\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00629\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 32-\/bit\ MinGW\ wants\ ESP\ to\ be\ 16-\/byte\ aligned,\ but\ this\ is\ not\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00630\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Windows\ ABI\ and\ VC++\ as\ well\ as\ Windows\ DLLs\ don't\ maintain\ that\ invariant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00631\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ As\ a\ result,\ enabling\ SSE2\ on\ 32-\/bit\ MinGW\ is\ dangerous\ when\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00632\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ simultaneously\ enabling\ "{}-\/mstackrealign"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00633\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00634\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ See\ https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/81\ for\ more\ information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00635\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00636\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ So\ default\ to\ no\ SSE2\ on\ 32-\/bit\ MinGW.\ If\ you've\ read\ this\ far\ and\ added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00637\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/mstackrealign\ to\ your\ build\ settings,\ feel\ free\ to\ \#define\ STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00638\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00639\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00640\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00641\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)\ \&\&\ (defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET)\ ||\ defined(STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET))}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00882\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00883\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ stb\_image\ uses\ ints\ pervasively,\ including\ for\ offset\ calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00884\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ therefore\ the\ largest\ decoded\ image\ size\ we\ can\ support\ with\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00885\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ current\ code,\ even\ on\ 64-\/bit\ targets,\ is\ INT\_MAX.\ this\ is\ not\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00886\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ significant\ limitation\ for\ the\ intended\ use\ case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00887\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00888\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ we\ do,\ however,\ need\ to\ make\ sure\ our\ size\ calculations\ don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00889\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ overflow.\ hence\ a\ few\ helper\ functions\ for\ size\ calculations\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00890\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ multiply\ integers\ together,\ making\ sure\ that\ they're\ non-\/negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00891\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ no\ overflow\ occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00892\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00893\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ return\ 1\ if\ the\ sum\ is\ valid,\ 0\ on\ overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00894\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ negative\ terms\ are\ considered\ invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00895\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structa}{a}},\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00896\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00897\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (b\ <\ 0)\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00898\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ now\ 0\ <=\ b\ <=\ INT\_MAX,\ hence\ also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00899\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 0\ <=\ INT\_MAX\ -\/\ b\ <=\ INTMAX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00900\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ And\ "{}a\ +\ b\ <=\ INT\_MAX"{}\ (which\ might\ overflow)\ is\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00901\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ same\ as\ a\ <=\ INT\_MAX\ -\/\ b\ (no\ overflow)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00902\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structa}{a}}\ <=\ INT\_MAX\ -\/\ b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00903\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00904\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00905\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ returns\ 1\ if\ the\ product\ is\ valid,\ 0\ on\ overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00906\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ negative\ factors\ are\ considered\ invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00907\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structa}{a}},\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ b)}

\DoxyCodeLine{01817\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ simple\ implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01818\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ doesn't\ support\ delayed\ output\ of\ y-\/dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01819\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ simple\ interface\ (only\ one\ output\ format:\ 8-\/bit\ interleaved\ RGB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01820\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ doesn't\ try\ to\ recover\ corrupt\ jpegs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01821\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ doesn't\ allow\ partial\ loading,\ loading\ multiple\ at\ once}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01822\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ still\ fast\ on\ x86\ (copying\ globals\ into\ locals\ doesn't\ help\ x86)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01823\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ allocates\ lots\ of\ intermediate\ memory\ (full\ size\ of\ all\ components)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01824\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ non-\/interleaved\ case\ requires\ this\ anyway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01825\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ allows\ good\ upsampling\ (see\ next)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01826\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ high-\/quality}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01828\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ quality\ integer\ IDCT\ derived\ from\ IJG's\ 'slow'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01829\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ performance}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06126\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ RLE\ as\ used\ by\ .PSD\ and\ .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06127\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Loop\ until\ you\ get\ the\ number\ of\ unpacked\ bytes\ you\ are\ expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06128\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ Read\ the\ next\ source\ byte\ into\ n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06129\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ If\ n\ is\ between\ 0\ and\ 127\ inclusive,\ copy\ the\ next\ n+1\ bytes\ literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06130\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ Else\ if\ n\ is\ between\ -\/127\ and\ -\/1\ inclusive,\ copy\ the\ next\ byte\ -\/n+1\ times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06131\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ Else\ if\ n\ is\ 128,\ noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06132\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06133\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{06134\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ RLE-\/compressed\ data\ is\ preceded\ by\ a\ 2-\/byte\ data\ count\ for\ each\ row\ in\ the\ data,}}
